\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{DEPRECATED\ APIS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{===============}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{Version\ 0.9.0\ deprecated\ the\ per-\/sample\ reading\ and\ seeking\ APIs\ and\ replaced\ them\ with\ versions\ that\ work\ on\ the\ resolution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{of\ a\ PCM\ frame\ instead.\ For\ example,\ given\ a\ stereo\ WAV\ file,\ previously\ you\ would\ pass\ 2\ to\ drwav\_read\_f32()\ to\ read\ one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{PCM\ frame,\ whereas\ now\ you\ would\ pass\ in\ 1\ to\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32().\ The\ old\ APIs\ would\ return\ the\ number\ of\ samples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{read,\ whereas\ now\ it\ will\ return\ the\ number\ of\ PCM\ frames.\ Below\ is\ a\ list\ of\ APIs\ that\ have\ been\ deprecated\ and\ their}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{replacements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_read()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_read\_s16()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_read\_f32()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_read\_s32()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_seek\_to\_sample()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_seek\_to\_pcm\_frame()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_write()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_write\_pcm\_frames()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_open\_and\_read\_s16()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_open\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_open\_and\_read\_f32()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_open\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_open\_and\_read\_s32()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_open\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_open\_file\_and\_read\_s16()\ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_open\_file\_and\_read\_f32()\ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_open\_file\_and\_read\_s32()\ \ \ -\/>\ drwav\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_s16()\ -\/>\ drwav\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_f32()\ -\/>\ drwav\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_s32()\ -\/>\ drwav\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav::totalSampleCount\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drwav::totalPCMFrameCount}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{Rationale:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ 1)\ Most\ programs\ will\ want\ to\ read\ in\ multiples\ of\ the\ channel\ count\ which\ demands\ a\ per-\/frame\ reading\ API.\ Per-\/sample}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ reading\ just\ adds\ complexity\ and\ maintenance\ costs\ for\ no\ practical\ benefit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ 2)\ This\ is\ consistent\ with\ my\ other\ decoders\ -\/\ dr\_flac\ and\ dr\_mp3.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{These\ APIs\ will\ be\ removed\ completely\ in\ version\ 0.10.0.\ You\ can\ continue\ to\ use\ drwav\_read\_raw()\ if\ you\ need\ per-\/sample}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{reading.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{USAGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{=====}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ is\ a\ single-\/file\ library.\ To\ use\ it,\ do\ something\ like\ the\ following\ in\ one\ .c\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ DR\_WAV\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \#include\ "{}dr\_wav.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ can\ then\ \#include\ this\ file\ in\ other\ parts\ of\ the\ program\ as\ you\ would\ with\ any\ other\ header\ file.\ Do\ something}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{like\ the\ following\ to\ read\ audio\ data:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\ wav;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ if\ (!drwav\_init\_file(\&wav,\ "{}my\_song.wav"{}))\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Error\ opening\ WAV\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_int32*\ pDecodedInterleavedSamples\ =\ malloc(wav.totalPCMFrameCount\ *\ wav.channels\ *\ sizeof(drwav\_int32));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ size\_t\ numberOfSamplesActuallyDecoded\ =\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s32(\&wav,\ wav.totalPCMFrameCount,\ pDecodedInterleavedSamples);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_uninit(\&wav);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ can\ also\ use\ drwav\_open()\ to\ allocate\ and\ initialize\ the\ loader\ for\ you:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav*\ pWav\ =\ drwav\_open\_file("{}my\_song.wav"{});}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ if\ (pWav\ ==\ NULL)\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Error\ opening\ WAV\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ...}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ you\ just\ want\ to\ quickly\ open\ and\ read\ the\ audio\ data\ in\ a\ single\ operation\ you\ can\ do\ something\ like\ this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ unsigned\ int\ channels;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ unsigned\ int\ sampleRate;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_uint64\ totalPCMFrameCount;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ float*\ pSampleData\ =\ drwav\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32("{}my\_song.wav"{},\ \&channels,\ \&sampleRate,\ \&totalPCMFrameCount);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ if\ (pSampleData\ ==\ NULL)\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Error\ opening\ and\ reading\ WAV\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_free(pSampleData);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ examples\ above\ use\ versions\ of\ the\ API\ that\ convert\ the\ audio\ data\ to\ a\ consistent\ format\ (32-\/bit\ signed\ PCM,\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{this\ case),\ but\ you\ can\ still\ output\ the\ audio\ data\ in\ its\ internal\ format\ (see\ notes\ below\ for\ supported\ formats):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ size\_t\ samplesRead\ =\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames(\&wav,\ wav.totalPCMFrameCount,\ pDecodedInterleavedSamples);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ can\ also\ read\ the\ raw\ bytes\ of\ audio\ data,\ which\ could\ be\ useful\ if\ dr\_wav\ does\ not\ have\ native\ support\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{a\ particular\ data\ format:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ size\_t\ bytesRead\ =\ drwav\_read\_raw(\&wav,\ bytesToRead,\ pRawDataBuffer);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{dr\_wav\ can\ also\ be\ used\ to\ output\ WAV\ files.\ This\ does\ not\ currently\ support\ compressed\ formats.\ To\ use\ this,\ look\ at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{drwav\_open\_write(),\ drwav\_open\_file\_write(),\ etc.\ Use\ drwav\_write\_pcm\_frames()\ to\ write\ samples,\ or\ drwav\_write\_raw()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{to\ write\ raw\ data\ in\ the\ "{}data"{}\ chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_data\_format\ format;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ format.container\ =\ drwav\_container\_riff;\ \ \ \ \ //\ <-\/-\/\ drwav\_container\_riff\ =\ normal\ WAV\ files,\ drwav\_container\_w64\ =\ Sony\ Wave64.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ format.format\ =\ DR\_WAVE\_FORMAT\_PCM;\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ <-\/-\/\ Any\ of\ the\ DR\_WAVE\_FORMAT\_*\ codes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ format.channels\ =\ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ format.sampleRate\ =\ 44100;}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{without\ any\ manual\ intervention.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ \textcolor{comment}{OPTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{comment}{=======}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ these\ options\ before\ including\ this\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ DR\_WAV\_NO\_CONVERSION\_API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Disables\ conversion\ APIs\ such\ as\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()\ and\ drwav\_s16\_to\_f32().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ DR\_WAV\_NO\_STDIO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Disables\ drwav\_open\_file(),\ drwav\_open\_file\_write(),\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00133\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00134\ \textcolor{comment}{QUICK\ NOTES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00135\ \textcolor{comment}{===========}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00136\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ Samples\ are\ always\ interleaved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00137\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ The\ default\ read\ function\ does\ not\ do\ any\ data\ conversion.\ Use\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32(),\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00138\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ and\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()\ to\ read\ and\ convert\ audio\ data\ to\ 32-\/bit\ floating\ point,\ signed\ 32-\/bit\ integer\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00139\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ signed\ 16-\/bit\ integer\ samples\ respectively.\ Tested\ and\ supported\ internal\ formats\ include\ the\ following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00140\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ Unsigned\ 8-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00141\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ Signed\ 12-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00142\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ Signed\ 16-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00143\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ Signed\ 24-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ Signed\ 32-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ IEEE\ 32-\/bit\ floating\ point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00146\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ IEEE\ 64-\/bit\ floating\ point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ A-\/law\ and\ u-\/law}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ Microsoft\ ADPCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ -\/\ IMA\ ADPCM\ (DVI,\ format\ code\ 0x11)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ dr\_wav\ will\ try\ to\ read\ the\ WAV\ file\ as\ best\ it\ can,\ even\ if\ it's\ not\ strictly\ conformant\ to\ the\ WAV\ format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00482\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00483\ \textcolor{comment}{Initializes\ a\ pre-\/allocated\ drwav\ object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00484\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00485\ \textcolor{comment}{pWav\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ [out]\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ pointer\ to\ the\ drwav\ object\ being\ initialized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00486\ \textcolor{comment}{onRead\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ [in]\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ function\ to\ call\ when\ data\ needs\ to\ be\ read\ from\ the\ client.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00487\ \textcolor{comment}{onSeek\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ [in]\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ function\ to\ call\ when\ the\ read\ position\ of\ the\ client\ data\ needs\ to\ move.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00488\ \textcolor{comment}{onChunk\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ [in,\ optional]\ The\ function\ to\ call\ when\ a\ chunk\ is\ enumerated\ at\ initialized\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00489\ \textcolor{comment}{pUserData,\ pReadSeekUserData\ [in,\ optional]\ A\ pointer\ to\ application\ defined\ data\ that\ will\ be\ passed\ to\ onRead\ and\ onSeek.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00490\ \textcolor{comment}{pChunkUserData\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ [in,\ optional]\ A\ pointer\ to\ application\ defined\ data\ that\ will\ be\ passed\ to\ onChunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00491\ \textcolor{comment}{flags\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ [in,\ optional]\ A\ set\ of\ flags\ for\ controlling\ how\ things\ are\ loaded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00492\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00493\ \textcolor{comment}{Returns\ true\ if\ successful;\ false\ otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00494\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00495\ \textcolor{comment}{Close\ the\ loader\ with\ drwav\_uninit().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00496\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00497\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ is\ the\ lowest\ level\ function\ for\ initializing\ a\ WAV\ file.\ You\ can\ also\ use\ drwav\_init\_file()\ and\ drwav\_init\_memory()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00498\ \textcolor{comment}{to\ open\ the\ stream\ from\ a\ file\ or\ from\ a\ block\ of\ memory\ respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00499\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00500\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ you\ want\ dr\_wav\ to\ manage\ the\ memory\ allocation\ for\ you,\ consider\ using\ drwav\_open()\ instead.\ This\ will\ allocate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00501\ \textcolor{comment}{a\ drwav\ object\ on\ the\ heap\ and\ return\ a\ pointer\ to\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00502\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00503\ \textcolor{comment}{Possible\ values\ for\ flags:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00504\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ DRWAV\_SEQUENTIAL:\ Never\ perform\ a\ backwards\ seek\ while\ loading.\ This\ disables\ the\ chunk\ callback\ and\ will\ cause\ this\ function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00505\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ to\ return\ as\ soon\ as\ the\ data\ chunk\ is\ found.\ Any\ chunks\ after\ the\ data\ chunk\ will\ be\ ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00506\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00507\ \textcolor{comment}{drwav\_init()\ is\ equivalent\ to\ "{}drwav\_init\_ex(pWav,\ onRead,\ onSeek,\ NULL,\ pUserData,\ NULL,\ 0);"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00508\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00509\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ onChunk\ callback\ is\ not\ called\ for\ the\ WAVE\ or\ FMT\ chunks.\ The\ contents\ of\ the\ FMT\ chunk\ can\ be\ read\ from\ pWav-\/>fmt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00510\ \textcolor{comment}{after\ the\ function\ returns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00511\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00512\ \textcolor{comment}{See\ also:\ drwav\_init\_file(),\ drwav\_init\_memory(),\ drwav\_uninit()}}
